##########################################
# 40858日军针对中国吞并军阀的部署 (JAP)
##########################################
event = {
	id = 40858
	random = no
	country = jap

	trigger = {
		atwar = yes
		OR = {       
		       NOT = { ai = chi }
		       NOT = { ai = chc }
                }
		NOT = { war = { country = CHI country = JAP } }
		NOT = {	event = 20 }
		OR = {
                        ispuppet = CHC
			NOT = {	exists = CYN }
			NOT = {	exists = CXB }
			NOT = {	exists = CHI }
			NOT = {	exists = CSX }
			NOT = {	exists = U01 }
			NOT = {	exists = U02 }
                        alliance = { country = chi country = eng }
                        alliance = { country = chi country = ger }
			AND = {
				event = 40816 #西安事变停止内战
				exists = CHC
				NOT = { ai = CHC }
				atwar = chc
			}
			AND = {
				event = 40816 #西安事变停止内战
				exists = CHI
				NOT = { ai = CHI }
				war = { country = CHI country = CHC }
			}
			owned = { province = 1205 data = CHC } #北平
			owned = { province = 1216 data = CHC } #济南
			owned = { province = 1209 data = CHC } #大同
			owned = { province = 1225 data = CHC } #太原
			owned = { province = 1226 data = CHC } #长治
		}
	}

	name = "日军针对中国吞并军阀的部署 "
	style = 2	

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1938 }

	action_a = {
		name = "ok"
		command = { type = ai_prepare_war which = CHI }
		command = { type = ai_prepare_war which = CSX }
		command = { type = ai_prepare_war which = CGX }
		command = { type = ai_prepare_war which = CHC }
		command = { type = ai_prepare_war which = U01 }
		command = { type = ai_prepare_war which = U02 }

		command = { type = dissent value = -10 }
		command = { type = belligerence which = JAP value = -50 } #The DoWs above is for free
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = 2 }
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 2 }
		command = { type = manpowerpool value = 500 }

		command = { type = add_corps which = "支那战区军团 " value = land where = 1203 }
		command = { type = add_division value = hq }
		command = { type = add_division value = armor when = 1 where = sp_artillery }
		command = { type = add_division value = armor when = 1 where = sp_artillery }
		command = { type = add_division value = motorized when = 56  }
		command = { type = add_division value = motorized when = 56  }
		command = { type = add_division value = motorized when = 56  }
		command = { type = add_division value = mechanized when = 36 where = light_armor_brigade }
		command = { type = add_division value = mechanized when = 36 where = light_armor_brigade }
		command = { type = add_division value = mechanized when = 36 where = light_armor_brigade }
		command = { type = add_division value = cavalry when = 2 where = armored_car }
		command = { type = add_division value = cavalry when = 2 where = armored_car }
		command = { type = add_division value = cavalry when = 2 where = armored_car }

		command = { type = trigger which = 21 }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 20 }
	}
}

	style = 2

	offset = 10
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1945 }

		name = "此举有助于进一步完成征服！ " #Prepare better action name

		command = { type = supplies value = 100 }
		command = { type = belligerence which = JAP value = 10 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 601500
	random = no
	country = JAP
	
	decision = { atwar = yes }

	decision_trigger = { 
            supplies = 5000
            OR = {
			    NOT = { motorized = { country = JAP value = 20 } }
			    NOT = { mechanized = { country = JAP value = 10 } }
	            NOT = { control = { province = 1235 data = CHI } }
                     }
        }
		
	trigger = {  atwar = yes
	        supplies = 5000
            OR = {
			    NOT = { motorized = { country = JAP value = 20 } }
			    NOT = { mechanized = { country = JAP value = 10 } }
	            NOT = { control = { province = 1235 data = CHI } }
                     }
        }

	name = "三联制改革：开始 "
	desc = "随着战争的深入，日军越来越发现原有的２旅团４联队的师团编 制愈发缺乏机动与灵活性。新组建的师团多已改建为国际通行的 “三联制”师团，３８年开始，原有的常备师团也开始进行三联 制改编。 "
	style = 2
	picture = "jieguanSH"

	date = { day = 1 month = 10 year = 1939 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = 12 year = 1945 }

	action_a = {
		name = "天皇板载！"
		command = { type = supplies value = 20000 }
		command = { type = oilpool value = 20000 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 63900  }
		command = { type = trigger which = 60150  }
	}
}

	id = 40700
	random = no
	country = JAP

	trigger = {
		government = fascist
	}

	name = "山下报告 "
	desc = "在对德国的官方访问期间，山下将军和日本驻德大使，大岛浩少 将进行了会谈。他们提交了一份详细描述德国先进技术的综合报 告。 "
	style = 2
	picture = "40700_yamashita_report"

	date = { day = 1 month = february year = 1936 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 20 month = february year = 1936 }

	action_a = {
		name = "立刻研究报告 "
		command = { type = dissent value = 2 }	
        command = { type = event which = 40702 where = JAP when = 30 }
	}	
}
event = {
	id = 40702
	random = no
	country = JAP

	name = "对山下报告的研究 "
	desc = "在仔细研究之后，日本军事技术的不足是显而易见的了。为了能 够分享德国先进的技术，我们必须拉近两国之间的友谊。 "
	style = 2
	picture = "40702_analysis_yamashita_report"

	action_a = {
		name = "派遣外交官员改善与德国的关系，并进行贸易会谈 "
		command = { type = money value = -500 }
        command = { type = event which = 40704 where = JAP when = 20 }
	}	
}

	id = 40704
	random = no
	country = JAP

	name = "与德国的外交谈判进展顺利 "

	style = 2
	picture = "40704_negociations_with_germany"

	action_a = {
		name = "ok"

		command = { type = event which = 40703 where = GER when = 9 }
	}	
}

#########################################################################
#  The 2-2-6 incident (Japan)
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 1
	random = no
	country = JAP
	
    name = "昭和维新--二二六兵变 "	
    desc = EVT_1_DESC
	style = 2
	picture = "226"

	date = { day = 25 month = february year = 1936 }

	action_a = {
		ai_chance = 75
		name = EVT_1_ACTA
		command = { type = dissent value = 1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = -1 }
		command = { type = set_domestic which = democratic value = 3 }
		command = { type = set_domestic which = political_left value = 4 }
		command = { type = domestic which = freedom value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		ai_chance = 25
		name = EVT_1_ACTB
		command = { type = dissent value = 10 }
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = 1 }  #  NOTE: The B choice effects are stronger than A by design
		command = { type = domestic which = democratic value = -3 }      #  This represent a greater shift towards the military and
		command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = -3 }  #  right wing control.
		command = { type = domestic which = freedom value = -3 }
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = -1 }
		command = { type = headofstate which = 5001 }
		command = { type = headofgovernment which = 5033 }
		command = { type = foreignminister which = 5053 }
		command = { type = armamentminister which = 5080 }
		command = { type = ministerofsecurity which = 5105 }
		command = { type = ministerofintelligence which = 5134 }
		command = { type = chiefofstaff which = 5007 }
		command = { type = chiefofarmy which = 5008 }
		command = { type = chiefofnavy which = 5172 }
		command = { type = chiefofair which = 5183 }
		command = { type = relation which = SOV value = -20 }
		command = { type = relation which = CHI value = -20 }
	}

# 1000094-95 新加坡英国守军投降事件组 (JAP、ENG) (by Civdemof)
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 1000094
	country = JAP
	random = no
	
	decision = {
	   control = { province = 1353 data = ENG } #新加坡
	   war = { country = ENG country = JAP }
	}

	decision_trigger = { 
        OR = {
               war = { country = ENG country = JAP }
               NOT = { division_exists = { type = 12700 id = 11 }}
	        }
		control = { province = 1353 data = ENG } #新加坡
		OR = {
		       control = { province = 3738 data = -3 } #新山
		       control = { province = 3747 data = -3 } #廖内群岛
	        }
	}
			
	trigger = {
        OR = {
               war = { country = ENG country = JAP }
               NOT = { division_exists = { type = 12700 id = 11 }}
	        }
		control = { province = 1353 data = ENG } #新加坡
		OR = {
		       control = { province = 3738 data = -3 } #新山
		       control = { province = 3747 data = -3 } #廖内群岛
	        }
	}

	name = "新加坡守军请求投降 "
	desc = "日军沿马来半岛南下，进攻号称“东方第一要塞”的著名军港新 加坡。１９４２年２月１５日，日军对新加坡市区的猛烈炮轰， 英军部队开始瓦解，英军指挥部于１５日上午开会决定投降。英 军司令珀西瓦尔中将在当天下午，向日军总指挥山下奉文签署无 条件投降书。英国守军约１０万人向约５万日军缴械。战役中， 日军死亡１７１３人，受伤３３７８人。 "
	style = 2
	picture = "british_pacific_defeat"

	date = { day = 5 month = january year = 1942 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1945 }

	action_a = {
		name = "兵不血刃 "
		command = { type = remove_division which = 12700 value = 11 } #新加坡防卫部队
		command = { type = supplies value = -1000 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 1000095 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 43
	random = no
	country = JAP

	name = "日本投降谈判 "
	desc = EVT_43_DESC
	style = 0
	picture = "JAP_surrender"

	trigger = {
	        NOT = { war = { country = JAP country = GER }}
	        OR = { 
		        war = { country = JAP country = USA }
		        war = { country = JAP country = SOV }
		}
		OR = {
			lost_national = { country = JAP value = 75 }
			OR = {
			        control = { province = 1184 data = -2 }
			        lost_national = { country = JAP value = 55 }
			}
			AND = {																							# BHT1.5
				control = { province = 1193 data = -2 }												
				control = { province = 1322 data = -2 }	
				control = { province = 1199 data = -2 }		
			        lost_national = { country = JAP value = 55 }											
			}													
			AND = {																						# BHT1.5
				control = { province = 1390 data = -2 }												
				control = { province = 1322 data = -2 }	
				control = { province = 1199 data = -2 }	
				control = { province = 1193 data = -2 }		
			        lost_national = { country = JAP value = 55 }											
			}													
		}
	}

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1940 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action_a = {
		ai_chance = 99
		name = EVT_43_ACTA
		command = { type = trigger which = 3729 } 
		command = { type = trigger which = 2666 } 
	}

		ai_chance = 1
		name = EVT_43_ACTB
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
		command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = freedom value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = democratic value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }

		command = { type = sleepevent which = 45 }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 135 } # BHT1.5
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 136 } # BHT1.5
	}
}
